And here you are not thirsty, troubled by the (sultry sweltering) sun
Yet Shaitan whispered (and aroused) doubts in his mind saying, "Oh Adam, shall I show you the tree of immortality, and the domain that has no demise
Both of them _ (Adam and his wife) _ ate its fruit and their genitalia became visible to them. With the leaves of the Garden of Eden they began to cover themselves. Adam disobeyed his Lord and went astray
Later, his Lord favored him, granted him forgiveness and guided him
(Allah) said, "Get down from here! Both of you _ (Adam and Shaitan)! You are each other´s enemy. Whoever follows the guidance _ when the guidance from Me arrives _ will not go astray, and will not be miserable
While a wretched (unwholesome) livelihood will be the lot of the one who turns away from My advice and warning. He will be blind when We round him up on the Day of Judgment
He shall say, "Lord, why did You raise me blind? I used to be endowed with eyesight
Allah will say, "Much the same as you ignored My signs when they came to you! Befittingly, today you are being ignored
This is how We chastise the one who exceeds the bounds, and ignores the signs of his Lord. The punishment of the afterlife is far worse and ever persisting
Many towns have We destroyed before them. Did that fact not teach them? They walk through those ruins! There are surely signs in it for those with intellect
The word of your Lord has been proclaimed! Had it not been, and if it wasn´t essential and for a specific period, (then their doom and demise would be instant)
Therefore, with patience bear their remarks and chant the praises of your Lord before the sun rises, before it sets, and during the night. Glorify Him in the morning and evening. Perhaps you will feel contented
Do not look (enviously) at the splendors of this life with which We have furnished some of their groups. It is (merely) to test them. The grants of your Lord (in the afterlife) are far better and ever lasting
Bid your family to observe the ´salat´, and stay steadfast upon it yourself. We do not seek sustenance from you. Indeed, We bestow sustenance. The final outcome hinges on piety
They say, "Why did he not bring us a sign?" Did clear proofs _ those narrated in the earlier scriptures _ not reach them
Had We, prior to sending him (Muhammad, SAW), ruined them with a disaster, they would have complained, "Our Lord, if only You had sent us a messenger, we would have followed Your signs instead of being disgraced and humiliated
Say, "Each (soul) is in a state of waiting. You wait, too! Soon you will find out who is on the right path, and well-guided
Their reckoning has drawn closer, but people are turning away in unmindful ignorance
When a fresh narrative from their Lord reaches them, they (barely) hear it, then they resume their pastimes
Their minds absorbed in pleasures, the evil doers whisper under their breaths, "Isn´t he just a human being like you all? Will you then, succumb to his magic knowingly
The messenger said, "My Lord knows everything uttered in the heavens and on earth. He is the All-hearing and the All-knowing
And they said, "Vague meaningless dreams, or he has made it up, or he is a poet. Else, let him present to us a miracle like the earlier (messengers) did
Those towns _ the ones We destroyed in the past _ had also failed to believe. So now, will they believe
We have always commissioned men (as messengers) and sent revelations to them, even before your time. Should you not know (this fact), ask the people of the scriptures
We did not fashion their physiques, so as to enable them to live without food, nor did they live forever
Then, We fulfilled Our pledge and rescued them, and those whom We wished. We destroyed those who had exceeded their limits
We have sent you this book. In it are narrations about your own self. So why do you not understand
Many towns have We dashed into fragments. They were evil! Then We brought other nations in their place
When they experienced Our power, they suddenly began to flee
Do not run away! Return to your homes and the luxurious comforts you were given. You will be called (to account)
They said, "Misery to us! We surely were evil
They kept saying that right until We turned them into the plucked out harvest
We did not create the heavens and the earth and everything in between as an amusement (and a pastime)
Had We wanted just to have fun, and if We were (given to) doing that, We would have done so all by Ourselves
On the contrary, We run the truth against falsehood, over which it triumphs. In time, the falsehood is bound to come to naught! Misery to you for what you attribute
Every living being in the heavens and on earth belongs to Him, and no one in His presence _ either out of pride or regret _ shies away from worshipping Him
All day and all night, they chant His praises. They do not relent
Have they accepted other gods on the earth? Do those other gods bring the dead back to life
The heavens and the earth would run into chaos had there been other gods beside Allah. Exalted is Allah, the Lord of the heavenly throne, far above what they utter
He is not answerable for His actions, while all others are (to Him)
Have they accepted other gods beside Him? Say, "Present your proof! Here is this reminder (the Qur´an) for those with me, and there are the scriptures for those before me." Most people actually do not know the truth, and so they ignore
Never was there a messenger before you to whom We did not reveal, "There is no god except Me, so worship Me (exclusively)
They say, "Rehman has adopted a son!" Glorified is He! Rather, they are all (just His) honored servants
They dare not initiate an audience with Him, and they diligently carry out His orders
He knows everything that lies ahead of them and everything about their past. They do not intercede for anyone except for those He is pleased with. They are attentive! And stand in awe and reverence of Him
We will award hell to anyone amongst them who says, "I am a god besides Him." That is how We punish the transgressors
Do the unbelievers not consider the fact that the heavens and the earth were joined together? We split them asunder! And from water, We created every living being! Do they not believe (that)
We pitched mountains firmly on the earth, lest it makes them sway. (Between the mountains) We cut roads and paths, so they may find their way
And (for you), We deemed the sky to be a safe and secure ceiling. Yet, these are the signs they overlook
And He is the One Who created the night and the day, and the sun and the moon. Each is afloat in its orbit
We have never bestowed immortality upon any human, including you, (Oh Muhammad, SAW). So you will die! But will they live forever
Every living being must taste death! We put you through trials, and We test all of you with (different) things _ bad as well as good! Then, towards Us, you shall all return
When the unbelievers see you, they treat you with scorn, (saying), "Is he the one who speaks (ill) of our gods?" While they themselves are such a sort that they refuse to accept any mention of Rehman
Man is created hasty. Very soon, I will have you see My signs! Do not be in such haste
And they say, "If you are truthful, tell us. When will that promise (of the afterlife) come about
If the unbelievers could only imagine the moment when they will struggle in vain to ward off the fire from their faces and their backs! They shall have no help
It will come upon them all of a sudden, and it will bewilder them. They will be unable to turn it away, and they shall have no respite (another chance)
During earlier times, too, they made fun of the messengers. But the mockery came back to haunt (and surround) those who used to mock
Say, "Who will watch over you during the night and the day, and protect you against (the wrath of) Rehman?" No! In fact, they turn away from the remembrance of their Lord
Or do they have other gods to guard them against Us? Those ´gods´ are unable to help even their own selves. Nor can they be guarded against Us
Rather, We had them and their forefathers enjoy (life) till they grew old. Do they not notice? We keep on shrinking the land from all sides. So then, can they triumph
Say, "The fact is, by this revelation I warn you!" But the deaf do not hear what they are being warned against
Even if a whiff of Our punishment were to hit them, they would surely cry out, "Oh misery to us, we were indeed the evil doers
We will indeed bring out the scales of justice on the Day of Judgment. No soul shall be wronged a bit. We will bring out (into focus) all deeds, even those (insignificant enough to be) worth a tiny bit of a mustard seed. And Our presence shall suffice to hold the reckoning
We had indeed granted Musa and Haroon the proof, the illuminating light and the (right) advice for those who fear
Those who fear their unseen Lord and dread the hour of judgment
This (Qur´an), now, is the blessed narration We have sent! So then, are you refusing to acknowledge it
Much earlier, We granted Ibraheem the maturity of mind
When he once said to his father and his people, "What are these statues you are worshipping so devoutly
They replied, "We found our forefathers praying to them
Said, "Surely, you and your forefathers were gravely misguided
They said, "Are you expressing your real views or are you just kidding
Indeed not! Your Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth, the One Who brought them into being. I bear witness to this (Truth)
Said, "I swear by Allah, I have plans for your idols when you go away and leave them
So he battered them to pieces, except the one most prominent. Maybe they would turn to it
They said, "Who did this to our gods? He is really very cruel
Some said, "We heard a lad called Ibraheem talking about them
They said, "Bring him out to face the people. So they may observe (his fate)
They asked, "Did you do that to our gods, oh Ibraheem
Said, "Rather, this one, their chief did that! Therefore, ask them if they can talk
They felt a pinch of conscience and (their inner voice) said, "Really, it is you who is being unjust
But they brushed that thought aside and said, "Of course, they do not talk! And you know it
He said, "Why then do you worship those besides Allah. They grant you no benefits, nor inflict any harm
Damn you, and those you worship beside Allah! Do you not understand at all
They cried, "Burn him at the stake! Rush to the aid of your gods! Act, if you will
We commanded, "Oh fire, simmer down, and let there be peace upon Ibraheem
They wanted to hurt him, but We caused them to be the real losers
Towards the blessed land, We had him and Loot escape. We had blessed it for the whole world
We gave Ibraheem a present: a son, Ishaq and (the grandson), Yaqub. We made each of them righteous
We made them both the patriarch _the leaders. As per Our instructions, they guided their people, and We revealed to them the acts of righteousness: the establishing of ´salat´ and the paying of "zakat". Both of them were Our devotees
As for Loot, We gave him wisdom and knowledge and rescued him from the people who committed the gravest of sins. They were indeed a very evil people
We admitted (Loot) into Our mercy; he was amongst the righteous
And prior to that, Nooh prayed to Us and We responded. We saved him and his family from a great torment
We came to his aid against a nation that had denied Our signs. They were an evil people, indeed. So We drowned them all _ every single one of them
And don´t forget Daood and Sulaiman as they sat in judgment, hearing the case of the field that had been overrun at night by goats of other folks. We were overseeing their judgment
We unveiled (the right ruling) to Sulaiman. We had granted wisdom and courage to both. For Daood, We had tamed the mountains and the birds. They used to chant praises with him! It was We Who did that
It was We Who taught him the art of making metal armors for you, so you may shield yourself during battles. But then, are you grateful
And for Sulaiman, (We tamed) the violent winds. Upon his orders they rushed towards the land We had blessed. We have the knowledge of all things
Groups of Shaitans (those We tamed), used to sea dive for him. Besides that, they performed other duties for him. We were the guardian over them
(And also) Ayub! He called his Lord, "An agony has befallen me while You are absolutely the most Merciful of all who show mercy
We heard his prayers, relieved him of his agony and reunited him with his family. We increased his family as a blessing from Us, and as an inducement for the worshippers
And (We also heard) Ismail, Idrees and Dhul Qifl. They were all patient men
And We admitted them into Our mercy. They were all righteous
And remember the one (who is well known because) of the fish. He left his town in exasperation, and he thought that We would fail to take him to task. Eventually, from the darkness he called, "There is no god but You. Exalted are You! Surely I was the offender
We responded and relieved his grief. That is how We relieve the believers
Zakaria called his Lord, (saying), "Lord, do not leave me alone (child less). You are the best of those who receive the heritage
We responded and granted him Yahya. We remedied (the condition of) his wife! All these (messengers) eagerly rushed towards the righteous acts, and prayed to Us with fear and longing. They all were humbly submissive to Us
(As also) that lady who had guarded her virginity. We breathed Our spirit into her body, and turned her and her son into a sign for the world
Listen! This human race of yours is really a single nation and I am your Lord, so worship Me exclusively
But they divided up their beliefs (and devotion) amongst themselves. All must return to Us
The efforts of anyone who performed the righteous acts _ provided he is a believer _ will not go unrecognized. Indeed, We are writing (everything) down
And forbidden it is for the town We have destroyed to bounce back
Until (the time), the ´Yajog´ and the ´Majog´ are let loose. They will begin to spring out from every hill
As the promise of that certainty _ (the reckoning) _ looms closer, the eyes of the unbelievers will be glazed and agape (with horror). They will cry out, "Oh misery to us, we stayed unmindful of this. Rather, we were the evil doers
Indeed! You, and those you used to worship besides Allah, shall serve as fuel for the hellfire, which you shall have to enter
Had they been gods, they would not end up here (in hell). Now, they shall stay here forever
There, wheezing (amid moans and shrieks) shall be their mode of breathing. In hell, they shall not hear anything (else)
But those, for whom the decree of joy and happiness had been issued by Us, will be spared the above fate
(In paradise), they shall not hear even the faint whimper of hell. Amid what they desire and yearn, they shall live for ever
That great anxiety will not afflict them. The angels will greet them (saying), "Today is your day, the one you had been promised
That day We will fold up the heavens like pages folded in a book. Then, We will begin the creation anew just as We had started it in the first instance. This is a promise incumbent upon Us. We are definitely going to fulfill (Our promise)
We, in fact, revealed in the "Zaboor" _ (the book revealed to Da´ood) _ following Our warnings, that only My righteous servants shall inherit the earth
In that, surely, is the message for the nation that prays
We have sent you only as mercy for the entire world
Say, "It has been revealed to me that your God, for sure, is that One true God. So then, are you ready to submit, and obey
If they turn their backs, say, "I have notified you _ all of you, together. I have no idea whether that which is being promised to you, (the day of Reckoning), is close by or far in the future
Of course, He knows that which is spoken aloud, as well as the thoughts you conceal
I do not know. It (the respite) maybe a trial for you, or else an enjoyment for a brief while
(Eventually), the messengers said, "Lord! Pass Your infallible verdict! And our Lord, the Beneficent, is our Advocate against every lie you utter
Oh you people! Fear your Lord! Indeed, the jolt of that hour (of Judgment) is a terrible thing
On that day _ (the Day of Judgment) _ you will see every breast feeding mother oblivious of her suckling infant! Every pregnant female would abort her fetus! And people would appear to be drunk although they would not be drunk! The punishment of Allah would indeed be that severe
Some people argue about Allah, although they have no knowledge. They tag along every defiant Shaitan
About whom it has been decreed, that he will lead astray anyone who abides by him, and that he will steer his flock straight into the torment of hellfire
Oh you people! Should you be in doubt about the resurrection, consider this: it is We Who created you (first) from dust and then (in stages) from semen to a clinging clot of blood, and then to a small chunk of flesh _ formed as well as unformed. (We tell you this) in order to explain to you the truth. In the womb, We keep installed whomever We want for a fixed time. Then, We bring you out as an infant, and let you obtain your full potential. Some of you die young while others are diverted to the age of weakness (and senility) _ the age when (once again) they know nothing after having learnt a few things. You observe the land dry and barren. Then, as soon as We send rain water down (it comes alive), it stirs, swells up and starts producing all sorts of delightful vegetation
That is so because Allah is the absolute Reality! And because He grants life back to the dead! He is capable of accomplishing everything
(Because it proves) that the hour of judgment is surely bound to come! No doubt about that! And that Allah will resurrect all (the dead) in their graves
Some people argue about Allah, although they do not have any knowledge, guidance or an illuminating book
Arching their necks conceitedly, they misguide people and drive them away from the path of Allah. Disgrace awaits them in this life, and on the Day of Judgment We shall have them taste the torture by fire
This is what your own hands have wrought. Surely, Allah does not oppress His servants
There are some people who worship Allah, but stay on the sidelines. If something good happens to them they are contented. But as soon as they are placed in a situation of trial, they undergo an about face and turn away. They lose out in this world, and also in the next! That, surely is a real loss
Instead of Allah, they pray to such deities that can inflict no harm, and award no benefits. That is surely the worst kind of misguidance
They pray to the one whose harm outweighs the benefits. Evil, indeed, is such a patron, and evil is such a companion
Allah will surely admit those who believe and act righteously into paradise. Rivers run right through it. Allah does what He wills
If anyone thinks that Allah will fail to help him (Muhammad, SAW) in this life and in the afterlife, then let that someone stretch his means to reach the heavens and traverse it. Let him see if his tricks can negate anything, including that which angers him
Thus, We send down the revealing verses. Surely, Allah guides whomever He wants
On the Day of the Judgment, Allah will surely settle the differences between the believers on the one hand, and the Jews, the Sabians, the Christians and the polytheists on the other. Allah is the Witness to all things
Do you not observe that everyone (and everything) in the heavens and on the earth falls prostrate before Allah: the sun and the moon, the stars and the mountains, the trees and the beasts, and a lot of people, too! Punishment has become warranted for many others (who do not prostrate). There is no honor for the one whom Allah humiliates. Undoubtedly, Allah does what He wills
These are the two rival groups _ (those who prostrate before Allah, and those who do not). They disagree about Allah. Garments made from fire have been readied for the unbelievers. Boiling water will be poured over their heads
Their skins and (even) their insides will melt away
Steel clubs shall be there (to restrain them)
Each time they emerge to escape the distress, they will be thrown right back into it. (They will be told), "Taste the torment of fire
(On the other hand), Allah will surely usher into paradise _ through which run the rivers _ all those who believe and do the righteous acts. They will don gold bracelets and pearls, and their garments shall be made of silk
They were led towards the pious speech (in this life), and towards the path of the One most Worthy of praise
We have deemed the holy mosque (in Makkah) to be an open place. There, residents and the visitors are equal! We will reserve a painful punishment for those who disregard that (equality) and are unfair, and those unbelievers who obstruct others from the path of Allah and the holy mosque
(Remember) We settled Ibraheem here, where the Kaaba now stands (with instructions): let there be no partners ascribed to Me in My house, and let it be rendered pure for those who perform ´Tawwaf´, and (as part of their prayer) stand, kneel and prostrate
Call all the people for Hajj. Let them arrive on foot or mounted on lean camels. They will respond and arrive from all directions
Let them witness the benefits (that exist) here for them, and during the specified dates let them invoke the name of Allah upon the sacrificial animals He has granted. Then, let them eat the meat and also feed the poor and the needy
After that, let them attend to their personal needs, complete the rites (of ´Hajj´), fulfill their vows and go around the ancient house, the ´Kaaba´ _ (the rite of tawwaf)
That was the purpose of ´Kaaba´! According to your Lord, honoring the obligations imposed by Allah is really better for you. It is allowable for you to eat the flesh of the (sacrificial) animals, except those you were informed about earlier. So, shun the filth of idolatry and steer clear of the false statement
(Forsaking all else and) without ascribing partners to Him, be a true believer in Allah. Ascribing partners to Him is like falling from the sky and being snatched up by the birds along the way; or being carried off by a tornado to be dropped off in a remote place
That is the reality! The sanctity for the symbols of Allah surely comes from the piety within one´s heart
You may benefit (from the sacrificial animals) for a while but then their place of sacrifice is near the ancient house
Different people were given different rituals of slaughtering and invoking the name of Allah upon the animals He provides. But the fact is your God is only one God, so submit (only) to Him! Give the glad news to those who surrendered to Allah´s will with humility
Such are they that their hearts are filled with fear when reminded of Allah. They bear with fortitude every distress afflicting them, establish ´salat´ and spend in Our path out of what We have provided
We have assigned the camels to be the ceremonial sacrificial animals for you. That is a blessing for you. Invoke Allah´s name upon them at the time of sacrifice. Then when their carcasses come to rest, eat their meat and offer it to the needy _ those who ask for it, as well as those who are reticent. This is how much We have tamed them for your sake! Perhaps you will feel grateful
Neither their flesh nor their blood reaches Allah, but your piety reaches Him. Thus, We tamed them for you, so (at the time of sacrifice) you may glorify Allah Who gifted you these animals So give the good news to those who do good deeds
Of course, Allah guards those who believe. Surely, Allah does not like any faithless ungrateful being
Permission to fight back is granted to those being attacked. For they have been wronged! Allah is quite capable of helping them
They have been driven out of their homes for no other reason except that they say, "Allah is our Lord!" Allah causes the fall of different people _ each by another. Otherwise, many places of worship _ like the monasteries, the temples, the churches and the mosques where Allah´s name is chanted a lot _ would be demolished. Allah will most definitely help those who help His cause. Of course, Allah is the Strongest and the most Powerful
Those who _ if We give them power (and authority) in the land _ would establish the ´salat´, pay the ´zakat´, enjoin the good and forbid the evil! The final outcome in all matters rests with Allah´s decision
So if they refuse to believe you, remember that prior to them, the nations of ´Samood´, ´Aads´ and Nooh also disbelieved
As also the nation of Ibraheem and that of Loot
So did the people of Madian. Musa, too, was accused of lying. So I granted the unbelievers a chance to redeem and reform. Finally, I grabbed them. How severe was My vengeance
In this manner, We destroyed many towns because of their evil ways. They are (in total ruin) turned upside down on their roofs. (So are) their abandoned wells and their lofty castles
Have they not moved about in the land? They are endowed with hearts to reason, and the ears to hear. Indeed, their eyes are not sightless. Rather, what is blind are their hearts within their chests
They taunt you to bring on the punishment at once. Allah does not go back on His words. But as you count, a day for your Lord equals a thousand of your years
To many a sinning towns, I granted (a respite and) an opportunity to redeem themselves. Finally, I nabbed them. Towards Me is their destination
Say, "Oh you people! The fact is, I am a candid warner for you
Thus, there is forgiveness and a generous sustenance for those who believe and do righteous acts
While those who strive to undermine Our signs (verses) will be the companions of hell
It happened to every messenger and prophet We ever sent. Whenever they desired (and received a verse) Shaitan put his own spin (interpretation) upon it. But Allah removes whatever Shaitan casts. And then He confirms and strengthens His verses. Allah is All-knowing and All-wise
(He does this) so that He may turn the work of Shaitan into a lure for those whose hearts are diseased and hardened. Surely, because of their malice and rancor, the evil doers (in their dissent) have strayed too far away (from the truth)
(This happens) so that those with knowledge may recognize it to be the truth from your Lord, that they may believe it and that their hearts may acquire reverence for it. Allah certainly guides those who believe towards the straight path
The unbelievers would keep on wrangling until the hour of judgment comes upon them suddenly, or the punishment creeps up on them on a day of disaster
The sole authority that day shall belong to Allah! He will settle all disputes between them. (As a result) those who believe and do good deeds would be in a serene and blissful paradise
But there will be a disgraceful torment for the unbelievers _ those who reject Our verses
Allah will definitely grant the exquisite riches to those who emigrate for the sake of Allah, and in doing so are slain or happen to die. Indeed, it is Allah Who is the best of the providers
Very definitely, He will admit them into the entrances (of exquisite palaces) which will delight them. Allah, indeed is the All-knowing and the Forbearing
If anyone retaliates because he was wronged unjustly, and seeks damages proportionate to his suffering (then he is justified), and if he is wronged again, then (he will find that) Allah will definitely assist him. Allah is indeed Oft-pardoning and much Forgiving
Because it is Allah Who wraps the night over the day, and rolls up the day over the night. Surely, Allah is All-hearing and All-seeing
Because only Allah is the absolute truth, while all others they pray to besides Him are false. Indeed, Allah is the Loftiest, and the Greatest
Do you not observe? When Allah sends water down from the sky the land becomes green with plants. Indeed, Allah is Well-acquanted (with everything), and the most Kind
Everything in the heavens and on the earth belongs to Him. Indeed Allah is free from want and is the most Praise-worthy
Do you not see? Allah has tamed everything on this earth for you. The ships sail in the sea by His command, and He withholds the sky so high, so it will not collapse upon the earth except by His will. Indeed, Allah is the most Forgiving and the most Kind
It is He Who gave you life, and He will give you death! Then, He will bring you back to life. Man, surely, is very ungrateful
We prescribed different rites of worship for each people. Regarding that, they really should not dispute you. Invite (them) towards the ways of your Lord. Certainly, you are well guided, and on the straight path
But if they choose to argue, say, "Allah is well Aware of what you are doing
On the day of reckoning, Allah will sit in judgment and resolve every disagreement you used to have
Are you not aware that Allah knows everything in the heavens and on the earth? That it is (recorded) in a book? And that is certainly easy for Allah
Besides Allah, they worship others about whom they have no knowledge. He has not revealed an approval for that. There shall be no helpers for the evil doers
As Our clear lucid verses are recited, you can see denial writ large on the faces of the disbelievers. They seem ready to pounce upon those reading Our verses to them. Say, "Shall I tell you about a greater distress? The fire, which Allah promises for those who fail to believe, and which is a monstrous destination
Oh you people! An example is being quoted. Listen attentively! Those you pray to besides Allah can create nothing _ not even a fly, though they may pool all their resources. (Worse than that) they are too powerless to rescue anything that even a fly might wrest away from them. Feeble are the seekers, and feeble are those being sought
They failed to honor Allah as much as He merits to be honored. Indeed, Allah is the Mightiest, and the most Powerful
Allah selects His messengers from among the angels as well as men. Surely, Allah is All-hearing and All-seeing
He knows all that lies ahead of them and all that is behind them. And towards Allah are all matters directed (for decisions)
Oh you who believe! Worship your Lord by kneeling and falling prostrate before Him; and do good deeds, so that you may prosper
And struggle all out for Allah. For, this struggle merits an all out effort. He has chosen you and has placed no hardship in your religion, the creed of your father, Ibraheem. Not only in this (Qur´an), but in the past, too, He had named you Muslims. (He chose you) so the messengers may witness your deeds (and testify), and you may witness the deeds of the rest of the people (and testify). So establish the ´salat´ and pay the ´zakat´ and hold on to your link with Allah. He is your Master! What an excellent Master! And what an excellent Ally
The true believers are the ones really successful
Those who pray with humility
And shun vulgarity
And discharge their obligation of ´zakat´
Those who (guard their chastity and) rein in their sexual urges
Except with their wives and those their right hands possess. For that, they deserve no blame
But, whoever lusts after anything beyond that is a transgressor
(And those) who honor their pacts and the trusts (held by them)
And those who maintain their ´salat´ watchfully
Such (believers) will be the heirs
They shall inherit the paradise where they shall live for ever
Certainly, We have created man from strands of clay
Then We made him into a drop (of sperm) lodged in an environment of stability
Next, We turned that drop of semen into a clot of blood and then changed that clot into a chunk of flesh. Next, We hardened that chunk of flesh into bones, and clothed the bones with flesh. Finally, We converted it into an altogether different being. Therefore, glorify Allah, the Best of the creators
Eventually, you would certainly die
And then, you will certainly be resurrected on the Day of Judgment
And surely, We have created seven systems (of heavens) over you. We are definitely not unmindful of the creation
We sent down water from the sky in measured amounts, and stored it in the land. We certainly have the ability to make it run dry
With it, We grow orchards of dates and grapes. You get plenty of fruits from the orchard as your livelihood
(We also produce) the oil tree that grows on Mount Sinai. It yields oil and makes a delicious meal
Indeed, there are lessons for you in your cattle, too. From their bodies We fetch you a drink (milk). You gain many benefits from them. You eat them, too
You mount them, and go aboard ships (over land and sea)
We surely sent Nooh towards his nation and he said, "Oh my people! Worship Allah! You have no god besides Him. Why do you not fear Him
But the elders, the leaders of his disbelieving nation said, "He is just a human like you, and he seeks dominance over you. Had Allah wanted, He would have sent angels. Never have we heard this from our forefathers
He is merely a man possessed. So just watch him for a while
He said, "Lord, help me against them. They have accused me of lying
Thus, We inspired him, "Build an ark under My supervision and instructions. When the floodwater comes bubbling out of the oven, bring on board a pair of each animal _ male and female, and also your family. But not those about whom Our word has already gone forth. Do not talk to Me about the evil doers! They shall all drown
When you and those with you have embarked, say, "All praise is for Allah Who saved us from the evil nation
Say, "Oh Lord, bring us ashore to a blessed land. You are the Best among those who lead ashore
In it, surely, is a sign. We are the One Who puts you through tests
After them, We raised another nation
We raised, from amongst their own, a messenger who said, "Worship Allah! You have no god besides Him! Why do you not fear Him
The elders and the leaders of his disbelieving nation who denied the (scheduled) meeting of the afterlife _ and whom We had granted luxuries in this life _ said, "He is only a man like you. He eats and drinks the same as you do
And, you will of course be the losers if you follow a man like yourself
Does he assert that after you die and become dust and bones you will rise (and live) again
What you are being promised is quite far fetched! Quite remote
Nothing but our existence in this world is real. Here is where we live and die; and we are not going to be resurrected
This man has merely invented a lie about Allah! We do not believe him
(The messenger) said, "Lord, help me! They have called me a liar
(Allah) said, "In a short while, they shall cut a sorry figure
Quite appropriately, a mighty blast seized them, and We churned them into trash. Thus, the nation of evildoers was dumped away
Then, after them We raised other nations
No nation can expedite its allotted time, nor prolong it
Then, We sent many messengers in succession. Every nation rejected their messenger when he came to them. So, We let them follow one after the other along the path of destruction. We reduced them to fables and folk tales. Any nation that refused to believe was tossed aside
Then, We sent Musa and his brother Haroon with Our signs, the clear and unmistakable proofs
To the pharaoh and his chiefs! But they displayed arrogance. They were a pretentious nation
They said, "Shall We believe these two men _ humans like us? Their people are our slaves
So they refused to believe (the messengers) and were destroyed
We certainly gave Musa the book, so that they may find their way
We deemed Jesus and his mother to be a test. We sheltered them on a plateau _ a peaceful place with a flowing stream
Oh messengers! Eat the wholesome food and perform the righteous acts. Indeed, I am well Aware of what you do
Surely, this nation of yours is a single nation and I am your Lord. So fear Me
But they divided up their religion into sects _ each one well pleased with its own beliefs
So, let them stay engrossed in their pastime for a while longer
What do they think? That when We increase their wealth and family
Are We rushing to bestow favors upon them? Of course not! They just don´t realize
Indeed, those who fear their Lord with anxiety and awe
And acknowledge the signs of their Lord
And do not associate partners with Him
And those who give charity _ whatever they can; their hearts tremble at the thought of returning to their Lord
They are the ones rushing towards all deeds of excellence, and they are the ones who surpass (excellence)
We do not burden anyone over and above his ability to bear. We have the book that declares everything truthfully. They shall not be wronged
But their hearts reeked of indifference (for the truth) and their deeds were different (from those of the believers). They carried on with their deeds
Until We grabbed their well-to-do (those living in luxury) with punishment. Then suddenly, they began to plead and entreat earnestly
Today, do not beg! Indeed, you shall receive no help from Me
My verses used to be read to you, but you used to turn your backs on them in disdain
You were arrogant! And during your night time escapades, you used to talk ill (of Our verses)
Did they not ponder upon the words (of Allah) at all? Did the messenger bring any thing that hadn´t ever come to their forefathers
Or is it that they do not know the messenger and therefore they reject
Or do they think he is mentally ill? Of course not! He has brought to them the absolute truth, but most of them have an aversion to the truth
Had the truth been made to follow their whims, the heavens and the earth and everything thereon would be ravaged and ruined. No, We have really brought them a reminder about their own selves. But, they are turning away from the narration about themselves
Or do you charge them a fee? The reward of your Lord is far better! He is the Best of the providers
Certainly! You are definitely calling them towards the straight path
And of course those who do not believe in the afterlife desire to drift away from that path
We may have mercy upon them and remove the distress afflicting them, but obstinately they continue to rove about in defiance
Indeed, We did grab them with distress, but they failed to surrender and adopt humility
Until We let loose upon them the severe torment! Then suddenly, they will lose all hope and wail in despair
It is He Who granted you the hearing, the sight and the heart (to feel and understand)! But seldom do you offer thanks
It is He Who scattered you on the earth; and you will be gathered together in His presence (again)
It is He Who gives life and death, and the changing of the night and the day is his (handiwork). Do you then, not understand
But in fact, their remarks are identical to those of their forerunners _ (the unbelievers of earlier times)
(They say) "Really? Will we really come back to life after we die and have become dust and bones
Of course in the past, too, the exact same promise was made to our parents and us. These are nothing but tales of people gone by
Say, "(Answer me this) if you know at all! To whom belongs this earth and everyone on it
They will respond, "Allah!" Say, "Then, do you not bear that in mind
Ask them, "Who is the Lord of the seven heavens, and who is the Lord of the Mighty Throne
They will say, "Allah!" Say, "Then, do you not fear Him
Say, "(Answer this), if you know at all! In whose hands is the destiny of all things? Who offers protection? And from whom there exists no escape
They will reply, "Allah!" Say, "Why then, are you being deceived
We did disclose the truth to them! But of course, they are the liars
Allah did not adopt a son. Nor is there another god along with Him. Else, each god would draw his creation apart and withdraw. Each would attempt to overwhelm the other. Exalted is Allah, far above what they say about Him
He knows the unseen and the manifest. And He is a lot loftier than those they associate with Him (as partners)
Say, "My Lord, in case You let me be the witness to the torment they have been promised
My Lord, do not let me be a part of the evil nation
We are indeed perfectly capable of letting you witness the punishment with which We have threatened them
(Oh messenger), rid the evil with that which is better! We are very well aware of what they utter
And say, "My Lord, I seek refuge with You against the evil promptings of the Shaitans
And I seek refuge with You, my Lord, so that they may not even come close (to me)
And when death comes to anyone of them, he will say, "My Lord, send me back
To the place I left behind! Perhaps, I will do good deeds (this time around)." Definitely not! These are mere words he utters. A barrier behind the dead (preventing their return to this life) shall exist till the day of their resurrection
Then, all links of kinship between them shall cease on that day. The day the trumpet sounds, they will not inquire about one another
Those whose scales (of good deeds) weigh heavier shall be successful
While the ones whose scales (of good deeds) weigh lighter have incurred for themselves a severe loss. In hell, they shall stay forever
Fire will scorch their faces. There, they will be gloomy and grave
Isn´t it true that My verses were recited to you, but you used to reject them
They will say, "Our Lord, our woes got the better of us. We are indeed, a blundering people
Our Lord! Take us out of here, if we ever commit (the same) again, we would really be evil
Allah will say, "Enough of that! Stay in it, and do not talk to Me anymore
Indeed, a group of Our servants used to pray, "Our Lord, We believe! Forgive us and have mercy upon us. You are the very Best of those who shower mercy
But you made them targets of ridicule. You mocked and scoffed at them with such intensity that it even made you forget Me (and My message)
Today I have rewarded them for their patience and perseverance! Indeed, they are the successful ones
Allah will ask, "How many years did you stay on earth
They shall reply, "We stayed only a day or part of a day. Ask those who are (given the task of) maintaining accounts
Allah will say, "You stayed for just a short while! If you had only realized
Did you think that We created you in vain? And that you will never be brought back to Us (for reckoning)
Exalted is Allah, the real Emperor! There is no god but He, the Lord of the Supreme Throne
Anyone who calls any other god besides Allah _ and for such an act he has no explanation _ will have to reckon with Allah. Surely, such unbelievers never succeed
And say, "My Lord, grant forgiveness and have mercy! Indeed, You are the very Best of those who shower mercy
It is We Who revealed this Surah, and it is We Who deemed it mandatory for you. In it, We have revealed clear unambiguous verses! Perhaps you will take counsel
Let both _ the man and the woman _ guilty of illicit sexual intercourse be punished with a hundred lashes each. If you really believe in Allah and the Day of Judgment, you will not let compassion hold you back from (implementing) the laws of Allah. A party of believers should be around to witness the punishment
The adulterer may marry none except an adulteress or a pagan, and the adulteress may be wedded only to an adulterer or a polytheist. It is prohibited for the believers (to marry an adulteress or let an adulterer marry the believing woman)
Flog those who accuse any of the chaste women (of committing adultery), but fail to backup (their charges) with four eyewitnesses. Flog them with eighty lashes, and thereafter do not accept their testimony ever again. Surely, they are the wicked ones
Except those who repent after that, and reform themselves. Allah is the most Forgiving and the most Merciful
And, if someone accuses his wife (of adultery) and has no witnesses other than himself, then let his testimony be treated as that of four witnesses. (Let him testify four times, saying each time that) he swears by Allah that he speaks the truth
And the fifth time, (let him say) that the curse of Allah be upon him if he was lying
And the wife´s punishment would be called off, if she testifies four times, (saying) that she swears by Allah, that he (her husband) is lying
And the fifth time (let her say) that the wrath of Allah may befall her if her husband is telling the truth
(You would have erred) had it not been for the favors of Allah and His mercy upon you; and also the fact that Allah is the most Forgiving and the Wisest
Those who brought up a slanderous lie (against the messenger´s wife) are but a small faction amongst you. Do not consider it bad for yourself. Rather, it is beneficial for you! Each of them is liable for the sin to the extent of his involvement. But the greatest torment is for the one among them who assumed the major responsibility
Why didn´t the believers _ men and women _ assume virtue for one of their own _ (a believer)? When you heard such a thing, why did you not say, "This is quite obviously a lie
Why did they not bring four witnesses (to back the allegations)? Since they failed to come up with the witnesses they, in the sight of Allah, are the liars
Allah has bestowed upon you His favors and His mercy, in this world and the life-to-come. Else, a great torture would have inflicted you because of the unrestrained gossip you indulged in
With your tongues, you spread (the lie), and with your lips you uttered that about which you had no knowledge. You considered the matter trivial, but according to Allah, it was very grave
When you heard it, why did you not say, "It is not proper for us to discuss such a thing! Exalted are You (Oh Allah), it is a treacherous slander
Allah cautions you against behaving like that ever again _ if you are really the believers
And Allah explains to you His verses clearly. Allah is the all-Knowing and the all-Hearing
A painful punishment _ in this world and in the afterlife _ awaits those who want sexual waywardness and obscenity to spread through the believers. Allah knows it (all) while you know nothing (at all)
(And it would have spread) had it not been for the mercy of Allah and His favors upon you. Allah is the most Gracious and the most Merciful
Oh you who believe! Do not emulate the example of Shaitan. Whoever follows the footsteps of Shaitan (should know) that he always exhorts the commission of obscene and vile deeds and the prohibited acts. The favors of Allah and His mercy are upon you. Otherwise, none of you could have ever acquired the purity of heart. But Allah purifies whomever He wants. Allah is all-Hearing and all-Knowing
The wealthy and the resourceful should not swear that they would withhold assistance from their needy relatives and the poor, nor from those who have left their homes for the sake of Allah! Rather, they should forgive and bear no malice. Wouldn´t you like Allah to forgive you? Allah is the most Forgiving and the most Merciful
Surely, cursed _ in this world and in the afterlife _ are those who level charges of immorality against the innocent and chaste believing women. There is a severe punishment for them
That day, their tongues, their hands and their feet would testify against them regarding what they used to do
That day, Allah will grant them to the full extent their rightful compensation; and they will know that Allah is the self-evident truth
Bad women are for bad men who deserve the bad women. Similarly, pious women are for pious men, who deserve the pious women. They are upright and absolved of what others babble about them. Theirs are the forgiveness, and a generous provision
Oh you believers, do not enter the homes other than your own; unless you seek permission from their occupants, and have saluted them. This is better for you. Perhaps, you will comply
Do not enter if you find no one at home, except when you have the (prior) permission to do so. Return if you are asked to go back. That is more appropriate for you. Allah is very well aware of what you do
It is not wrong for you to enter an unoccupied house in which you have your goods (wares and other interests). Allah knows what you declare and what you conceal
And ask the believing men to (be modest and) lower their gaze and maintain their chastity. That is righteous and better. Allah is quite familiar with what they do
Ask the believing women to lower their gaze, guard their chastity, and not leave bare their beauty and charm, except that which becomes apparent by itself. Ask them to pull their veil-cloths down across their bosom, and not show their adornments to anyone except their husbands, fathers, husband´s father, sons, husband´s sons, brothers and their sons, sister´s sons, their women, the female slaves they own, the men-servants too old to have erotic desires, and boys not yet old enough to have awareness of the carnal. Ask them not to stamp their feet hard, in order to display (and jingle the jewelry worn on their feet and other) hidden adornments (under their outer garments). Oh you believers! Turn _ all of you _ towards Allah in repentance. Perhaps you will prosper
And arrange for the single (but poor men and women) amongst you to marry the pious slaves and maidservants. If they are poor Allah may enrich them by His grace. Allah abounds in generosity and knowledge
Those lacking the means to marry should abstain until Allah enriches them by His grace. Write down for your slaves _ those who desire to work for their freedom _ (the terms of emancipation) if you know them to be worthy and able. Give them something from the wealth Allah has granted you. Do not _ to gain the worldly benefits _ compel your slave girls into prostitution, while they wish to remain chaste. For the slave girl compelled in this manner, Allah is the most Forgiving and the most Kind
We have revealed to you the clear unambiguous verses and the example of those gone by earlier, and (We have revealed) the right advice for the pious
Allah is the light of the heavens and the earth. An example of its brilliance: there is a lamp in a luminous niche. The lamp is in a glass which itself gleams like a radiant star. It is lit by the oil of the blessed tree _ neither from the West nor the East. The oil of the lamp is ready to glow by itself even without being kindled. The bright luminous light is atop another brilliant light. Allah guides towards this light whomever He wants and Allah quotes this parable for the people. Allah is knowledgeable of all things
Allah has favored the setting up of houses, where _ every morning and evening _ His name would be glorified and His praises chanted
Neither trade nor sale distracts (God-fearing) men from remembering Allah, establishing ´salat´ or paying ´zakat´. They are frightened of that day when the hearts will flip and the eyes will turn (white with horror)
So, Allah may grant them compensation consistent with the best of their deeds, and boost it further by His grace. Allah grants unlimited bounties to whomever He wants
The deeds of the unbelievers are like a mirage in a sandy desert. The thirsty believes he sees water, but finds nothing there when he comes closer. There, he does find Allah, Who will let him have his due. Allah is very swift in reckoning
(The condition of the unbelievers is) like darkness in the deep dark sea covered over by a huge wave, which is swarmed over by another tide. Up above are thick heavy clouds. (Total) darkness, one atop another! If one pulls out one´s hand, one could hardly see it. The one whom Allah deprives of light cannot obtain light elsewhere
Do you not observe? Everyone in the heavens and on the earth chants the praises of Allah. The birds fly in the sky with wings spread. Each being has learnt its own prescribed form of ´salat´, and its style of singing the praises of Allah! Allah is well aware of what they do
The domain of the heavens and the earth belongs to Allah, and to Allah is the return journey (of all humans)
Do you not observe? Allah shoves the clouds gently, and brings several of them together into a pile. Then you see raindrops falling down from it. From the mountains, He raises the hailstorm into the sky and rains it down. With it, He strikes those He wants, while He spares others. The lightning flashes (of the storm) almost blind the vision
Allah alternates the night and the day. Surely, there is a lesson in this for those with insight
Allah has created all creatures from water. Some creep on their bellies, some walk on two legs and some on all four. Allah creates what He wants! Indeed, Allah has power over everything
We have surely revealed the plain precise verses! Allah guides towards the straight path whom He wants
They (unbelievers) say, "We believe in Allah and His Messenger and we obey." But after that, some of them turn away. Those are not the believers
When they are called towards Allah and His messenger _ so he may settle their differences _ some of them reject and turn away
(However) if the truth is in their favor, they feign obedience and accept (the decision)
Is there a disease in their hearts? Or do they mistrust? Do they suspect that Allah and His messenger would treat them unfairly? Of course not! In fact, it is they who are unjust
The believers, too, are called towards Allah and His messenger, so He may settle their differences. Their outlook (in sharp contrast) is that they say, "We hear and we obey". Such, indeed, are the successful ones
Those who obey Allah and His messenger, fear Allah and do their duty, are indeed the triumphant ones
They swear so very solemnly that they would definitely leave home (and go forth into battle) if you ordered them. Say, "Do not swear! Obedience is what is required!" Allah is well Aware of what you do
Say, "Obey Allah and obey the messenger and if you turn away, then (remember that) the messenger is liable for the responsibility he bears, while you are accountable for your burden of responsibility. If you obey him, you would be led on to the right way. Apart from conveying the message clearly, the messenger has no further responsibility
Allah grants a guarantee to those of you who believe and perform the righteous deeds. He will most certainly appoint them the successors on earth, just like He appointed the people prior to you as successors. He will consolidate their way of life, much to their satisfaction. He will change their present state of insecurity and fear, into one of safety and peace. They would worship Me and would not associate anyone as My partner. Whoever disbelieves after this, is certainly wicked
Establish the ´salat´, pay the ´zakat´ and obey the messenger. So that you may be dealt with mercifully
Do not even doubt that the unbelievers can ever render (Allah) helpless on this earth. Fire will be their abode, which is indeed the worst of the destination
Oh you believers, let your slaves and young pre-puberty children seek permission (to come to you) during the following three times: before the morning prayer, at around noon when you undress (for a nap), and after the night prayers. These three timings are private! At other times, there is no harm either for them or you (to come unannounced). After all, you have to move about and see each other. Thus, Allah clarifies the verses for you. Allah is all-Knowing, all-Wise
Once your children attain puberty, let them seek permission (to enter your private chambers) just like other adults do. In this manner, Allah clarifies for you His verses. Allah is all-Knowing, all-Wise
It would not do any harm if the old ladies discard their veil cloth _ those who are past their childbearing age and do not expect to get married. But not in such a way that they display their charm! However, it is better for them to refrain (from discarding their veil-cloths). Allah hears all and knows all
There is no restriction upon the blind, the lame or the sick to eat (at anybody´s home); just as you are at liberty (either) to eat at your own home or the homes of your father, mother, brothers, sisters, maternal uncles and aunts and the paternal uncles and aunts. You may also eat at the homes in your possession or those belonging to your friends. There is no prohibition: you may eat alone or together. But when you enter the home, salute the people there with the noble and blessed greeting from Allah. In this manner, Allah clarifies the verses for you. Perhaps you would understand
The real believers are those who have faith in Allah and His messenger. On a collective mission with the messenger, they do not depart without asking leave. Those who seek permission before leaving are actually the ones believing in Allah and His messenger. (Oh messenger), if they ask your leave to go, in order to attend to any of their concerns, you may allow whomever you want and ask Allah to forgive them. Indeed, Allah is the most Forgiving and the most Merciful
Do not think that the call of the messenger is quite the same as an invitation from others amongst you. Allah is well Aware of those who _ using others as a cover _ slip away. Those who violate the commands of the messenger should beware lest a trial may inflict them, or a painful torment may come upon them
Listen good! Everything in the heavens and on earth belongs to Allah! He knows whatever course you are on. The day they are brought back to Him is when He will show them (the outcome of) their deeds. Allah is Knowledgeable about everything
Blessed is He Who revealed the criterion _ (the Qur´an) _ to His servant (Muhammad, SAW), so he may serve as a warner for the whole world
The domain of the heavens and the earth belongs to Allah. He did not beget a son, nor does He have a partner in His domain. He created everything, and then ordained its destiny in a precise manner
The other gods they accept besides Allah create nothing, and are themselves created. It is not within their means to harm anyone, or confer any benefits _ not even upon themselves. They have no ability to give death or life, or to resurrect the dead
The unbelievers say, "It is nothing but a lie that he has invented, and other folks have helped him with it." They have really brought about an unjust and false testimony
They say, "Tales of people long gone! He has written them down. (These tales) are dictated to him morning and evening
Say, "This Quran is revealed to me by the One Who knows all the mysteries of the heavens and the earth. Indeed, He is the most Forgiving and the most Merciful
They say, "What sort of messenger is this? He eats food and moves about in the bazaars. Why wasn´t an angel sent down with him to be a co-warner
Else, why was he not presented with a treasure? Why is it that he has no orchard to enrich him?" These unjust people remark, "You are merely following a crazy man
See! How they throw insults at you, and thus lead themselves astray! They are not able to find their way
Blessed is the One Who, if He wants, can grant you a much better garden than that, like the gardens with streams running right through. He can build you palaces
No! In fact, they refused to believe the hour (of judgment). For the one who rejects the hour, We have prepared a blazing fire
As the fire catches sight of them from afar, they will hear its sighs and sounds of fury
Bound together in chains, they will wail and beg for death as they are tossed into a cramped space (in the hellfire)
This day, do not just ask for a single death! Call for several deaths
Ask them, "Is this better? Or the eternal paradise which the pious have been promised?" It is their reward and their final destination
There, anything they desire shall be theirs; and there, they shall live forever. That promise is a definite obligation upon your Lord
That is the day He will gather them all; and also those they worship other than Allah. To them He will say, "Was it really you who made these servants of Mine go astray? Or did they stray from the path all on their own
They will say, "Glory be to You! It is not right for us to accept any patrons other than You! You had them and their parents enjoy plenty of comforts. But, they disregarded the warnings and became a doomed people
They (the false gods) will deny flat out then, what you are claiming (for them) now. Then, you would be unable to avert disaster or seek help. We will make the evildoers amongst you taste the tremendous torment
(Oh messenger)! Prior to you, too, every messenger We ever sent consumed food and moved about in the bazaars. We designed each of you to be a test for others. So, won´t you be patient? Your Lord is ever alert and watchful
Those not anticipating a meeting with Us said, "Why were angels not sent down for us? And why do we not see our God?" They deem themselves too important, and have been arrogant a great deal
One day, they will get to see the angels. But (the proceedings of) that day will not bring any good news for these criminals. The angels will say, "For you the good news is absolutely forbidden
We will bring out all the good deeds they have performed. Then, We will grind them into fine dust and blow the dust away
That day, the people of paradise shall have exquisite residences and the most peaceful resting places
That day, the sky and the clouds will split apart; and through it, angels shall descend in a continuous stream
That day, the sole and genuine authority shall belong to Rehman. That day will be tough for the unbelievers
That day, the evildoers will bite their hands in despair and say, "Oh misery! If only I had gone along with the messenger
Alas! My misfortune! If only I had not taken that one _ (the Shaitan) _ as a friend
He really made me disregard the advice when it came to me." Indeed, the Shaitan always betrays man in times of need
And the messenger will say, "My Lord, truly my people had forsaken this Qur´an
In this manner, We designated for every prophet an opponent from amongst the guilty. Your Lord suffices as a Guide and a Helper
The unbelievers say, "Why wasn´t this Qur´an revealed to him in a single stretch?" This was done in order that We may fortify your heart with it. It is revealed gradually and phrased elegantly
We responded to every objection they threw at you. We brought you the truth and the most excellent explanations
Gathered around the hellfire and shoved into it face down, would indeed be those who held the worst of beliefs and had strayed the farthest away from the path
We had surely granted Musa the book, and had appointed his brother Haroon as an assistant
We said, "Go to the people who have rejected Our signs." (Finally) We annihilated that nation completely
We drowned the nation of Nooh when they rejected the messengers! We turned them into an admonition for the whole world. For the evil doers, We have prepared a painful punishment
(Also for) the Aads, the Samoods, the people of ´Russ´ and several generations in between
We gave all of them the words of wisdom. Finally, We brought them to total ruin
They have surely passed by the town upon which was sent the most wretched rain. Did they not see it (coming)? But they did not expect the life after death
As soon as they see you, they make fun of you (saying), "Is he the one Allah sent as a messenger
He had almost wooed us away from our gods. But we stayed staunch upon them." As soon as they confront their punishment they will find out who had strayed farther away from the path
Did you see the one who took his own wishes and whims as his god? Can you then, (accept to) be in charge of his affairs
Do you think most of them listen, or ponder? They are like animals! Nothing more! In fact, they are (worse; they are) more astray from the right path
Do you not see how your Lord spreads out darkness? If He wanted, He could make it permanent! But He appointed the sun as a pilot (to drive away the darkness)
Thus We gently seize (the darkness) and gradually ease it away
It is He Who made the night don the decor that is fit for sleeping; and He made the sleep invigorating for you. He made the day a time to wake up
It is He Who sends the winds as heralds of His mercy! We send pristine water down from the sky
So that, with it We may bring the dead land back to life and quench (the thirst of) a great many cattle and people We have created
And We repeat this (feat) in their midst in various ways (and often enough) in order to impress upon them (the truth). But most people (being ungrateful) insist upon disbelieving
If We wanted, We could have raised a warner in every single locality
So, do not yield to (the demands of) the unbelievers, and strive against them relentlessly for the sake of this great struggle
It is He Who joined (the two) seas together. One is sweet and palatable, the other brackish and bitter. He has placed between the two of them a barrier _ an absolute restraint
It is He Who created man from water, then initiated two kinds of lineage of descent for him _ the paternal and maternal. Your Lord is Omnipotent
Besides Allah, they worship those who do not confer benefits upon them, nor cause them harm. The unbeliever always aids (Shaitan) against his Lord
We have sent you as a bearer of good news; and as a warner
Say, "In return, I do not ask you for a reward, except that whoever wants may adopt the path towards his Lord
Place your trust in the Ever-Living _ the One Who will never die, and chant His praises. He is sufficiently knowledgeable about the sins of His servants
It is He Who created the heavens and the earth and everything in between in six periods of time, and then mounted the throne. (He is) Rehman! Ask Him! He knows it all
When they are asked to fall prostrate before Rehman they say, "Who is Rehman? Shall we fall prostrate merely because you tell us to do so?" Thus, their hatred grows
Blessed is He Who created fortified spheres in the heavens and placed (in one of them) the great lamp _ (the sun) _ and the luminous moon
It is He Who makes the night and the day follow each other! A lesson for the one who wants to reflect, and wants to be grateful
The (real) servants of Rehman are those who carry themselves around in this world with humility and serenity. When accosted by ignorant ones they respond, "Peace
Those who spend nights (in prayers) standing and prostrating before their Lord
Those who say, "Oh our Lord, keep the torment of the hellfire away from us. Indeed, that torment is abiding and unyielding
Indeed, it is the worst place as an abode
They are neither extravagant nor miserly. While spending, they remain steady between the two extremes
They who do not pray to gods other than Allah, do not kill a being prohibited by Allah, unless mandated by justice, and do not commit adultery. Anyone indulging in these acts will receive punishment
His punishment will be doubled on the Day of Judgment, and he will stay there forever in a disgraceful despicable state
Except those who repent, believe and perform righteous acts. For such ones Allah will exchange their bad deeds with good ones. And Allah is the most Forgiving, the most Merciful
He who renounces (his evil ways) and performs the righteous deeds has indeed turned to Allah with true repentance
(The righteous are) those who do not bear false testimony. When they come across anything banal and indecent, they pass by it with dignity and grace
When reminded of the verses of their Lord, they do not stay inactive (and mute) like the deaf and the blind. (They listen and ponder)
Those who say, "Our Lord, grant us joy and bliss with our wives and children, and make us the models for the righteous (among our progeny to follow)
Those are the ones who will be rewarded with the exalted places (in paradise) in return for their patient persistence. They shall be greeted with the salutations of peace
They will stay there for ever! An excellent place to stay! An excellent abode
Say (to the unbelievers), "Unless you call my Lord and pray to Him, He would care nothing about you at all. But now, since you have rejected Him the torment will be yours forever
Ta, Seen, Meem
These are the verses of the vividly clear book
Would you then be overcome with sorrow because they do not believe
We can, if We want, reveal to them a sign from the heavens, which would cause their heads to bow down (in submission)
They turn their backs on every fresh reminder that ever comes to them from Rehman
They have now already rejected it (the Qur´an) and have made fun of it. But very soon the reality (and the effect) of their mockery will dawn upon them
Do they not look at the earth? We have caused all kinds of beneficial plants to grow on the land
In this, there is indeed a sign! Yet, most of them are not going to believe
And your Lord, indeed, is the most Powerful and the most Kind
(Tell them about the time) when your Lord summoned Musa, "Go to the evil-doing nation
The nation of the pharaoh! Do they not fear
Musa said, "My Lord, I am really afraid that they will reject me
My chest feels tight and my tongue fails to express. So, send for (my brother) Haroon
They have a charge (of a crime) against me. I fear that they will put me to death
(Allah) said, "Of course not! Go to them _ both of you _ with Our signs. Of course, We are with you listening (to everything)
So go to the pharaoh and say, "We are the messengers of the Lord of the entire universe
Therefore, send the children of Israel with us
The pharaoh said, "Did we not raise you up from an infant? And did you not spend a portion of your life with us
Yet, you committed that crime! That which you did! You are ungrateful
(Musa) said, "I did it then, when I was misguided
So I felt frightened and ran away from you. But my Lord gave me the commandments and appointed me a messenger
This favor you boast of conferring upon me is (nothing but the fact) that you have enslaved the children of Israel
The pharaoh asked, "And what is this Lord of the universe
Musa said, "The Lord of the heavens and the earth, and everything that lies between the two, if you want to be specific
The pharaoh said to those around him, "Did you hear that
(Musa) added, "Your Lord, and the Lord of your parents and ancestors
(The pharaoh) said, "This messenger of yours sent towards you is surely a lunatic
(Musa) continued, "The Lord of the East and the West and whatever lies between the two, if you were to understand
(The pharaoh) said, "I will have you rot in prison if you accept any god other than me
(Musa) said, "Even if I offered something definite (as evidence)
The pharaoh said, "Present it now, if you really mean it
(Musa) threw down the stick in his hand. Then, suddenly (and distinctly) it became a serpent
(He pulled his hand out of his armpit) and it suddenly appeared dazzling white to the viewers
The pharaoh addressed his courtiers saying, "He is surely a skilled magician
By the force of his magic, he wants to expel you from this land. Now, what do you recommend
They said, "Let him and his brother go back. Then, send your agents to the cities
They will summon every expert magician before you
At the specified time on the appointed day, the magicians were summoned
And the people were told, "Would you, too, come to the assembly
So that if the magicians triumph, we will follow them
The magicians came to the pharaoh and said, "There would surely be a reward in it for us, if we are victorious. Wouldn´t there
(The pharaoh) said, "Yes! In that case, you will become my close associates
Musa said to them, "Cast (your spell) whatever you have to
They cast their (spells on the) ropes and sticks and said, "By the power of the pharaoh, we will certainly triumph
Musa, too, threw his stick and it gobbled up all the illusions they had conjured up
The magicians fell down prostrate
They said, "We accept the Lord of the universe
The Lord of Musa and Haroon
The pharaoh said, "You dare to believe him before I could give you my consent. He must be your chief who has taught you the art of magic. You will soon come to know. Be sure, I will lop off your hand from one side and the leg from the other. After that, I will definitely crucify you (all)
They said, "It does not matter! We will surely return to our Lord
(They prayed), "We truly hope that our Lord will forgive our sins, (since) we are the first ones to believe
We sent revelation to Musa, "Slip away with My servants at night. You are surely going to be pursued
The pharaoh sent his agents to the cities to proclaim
They are just a handful of people
They have wrought our wrath (upon themselves)
And we are all here _ watchful and forewarned
(In this manner) We brought them out of their gardens, and spas
Their treasures and their fine residences
And We had the children of Israel inherit such things
They went after Musa and his followers at the crack of dawn
When the two opposing groups saw each other, the followers of Musa said, "We have been caught
(Musa) said, "Of course not! My Lord is with me! He will guide me, for sure
We instructed Musa by revelation, to strike the sea with his stick! The sea split; each portion stood like a huge towering mountain
We brought the other group closer
We rescued Musa and all those with him
And We drowned the others
Surely, there is a sign in that. Yet, most of them do not believe
It is your Lord Who is the most Powerful and the most Merciful
Narrate to them the story of Ibraheem
As he asked his father and his people, "Whom do you worship
They said, "We worship idols. And our devotion to them is constant
(Ibraheem) said, "Do they hear you when you call them
And do they help you, or hurt you
They said, "No! But we found our forefathers doing the same thing
(Ibraheem) said, "Did you ever notice (prudently) what it is that you worship
You and your parents of bygone days
Indeed, they are my enemies _ all of them; other than the Lord of the worlds
The One Who created me; and He guides
The One Who feeds me and quenches my thirst
When I fall sick, He restores my health
The One Who will give me death and will resurrect me after that
The One Who, I hope, will forgive my sins on the Day of Judgment
My Lord! Give me the wisdom and enroll me among the righteous
Grant me an honorable reputation with the future generations
And have me inherit the paradise full of favors
Forgive my father. He has surely gone astray
Do not disgrace me on the day they shall all be resurrected
The day when wealth and offspring will confer no benefits
Except to the one who comes to Allah with a sincere heart (free from doubt and disbelief)
The paradise will be brought close at hand for the righteous
And for the misguided the hellfire shall be made (conspicuous and) fully visible
And they will be asked, "Where are those you used to worship
Other than Allah? Are they helping you now? Are they helping themselves
They, along with the misguided, will be toppled into the hellfire
As well as the armies of Iblees _ every one of them
There, they will quarrel with each other, and say
By Allah, we were clearly wrong
When we thought of you as equal to the Lord of the universe
Criminals they were who led us astray
Now we have no one to mediate (and plead our case)
Nor do we have an intimate friend
If only we had another chance, we would surely be among the believers
There is surely a sign in that, but most of them do not believe
Your Lord surely is the One Who is the most Powerful and the most Merciful
The nation of Nooh rejected the messengers
Their brother Nooh said to them, "Do you not fear (Allah)
Surely, I am a faithful (and a reliable) messenger for you
Fear Allah and obey me
In return, I do not seek any compensation from you. My reward exists only with the Lord of the universe
So, fear Allah and follow me
They said, "Shall we believe you? Only the humble humdrum (and the despised) are following you
(Nooh) said, "I have no knowledge of what they used to do
My Lord alone has the prerogative to judge them, if only you could realize
I am not going to drive away the believers
I am a warner _ plain and simple
They said, "Oh Nooh, if you did not stop, you would surely be cursed and sentenced to death by stoning
(Nooh) said, "My Lord, my people have rejected me
Pronounce your judgment between me and them; and rescue me and all the believers with me
So We rescued him and those with him aboard a laden ship
And after that, We drowned all those (unbelievers) left behind
In that is a sign, of course! Yet, most of them do not believe
And your Lord, surely, is the One Who is the most Powerful and the most Merciful
The people of ´Aads´ rejected the messengers
Their brother Hood said to them, "Do you not fear (Allah)
Of course, I am a faithful (and a reliable) messenger for you
So fear Allah and obey me
In return, I do not seek any compensation from you. My reward exists only with the Lord of the universe
At every raised spot you construct high palaces in vain, and to no avail
You take up (residence in) large structures as if you will live (in them) forever
And when you assault, you land on your victim with a vengeance
Fear Allah and follow me
Fear the One Who has imparted the knowledge you possess
And has provided you the cattle and the sons
The gardens and the springs
In fact, I fear that a torture of a severe day might come upon you
They said, "It makes no difference to us whether you preach or discontinue your sermons altogether
These are merely the fantasies of the earlier folks
We are not going to be punished
So they rejected the messenger and We destroyed them. In this, is a sign of course! But most of them do not believe
And indeed your Lord is the One Who is the most Powerful and the most Merciful
The people of ´Samood´ rejected the messengers
Their brother Saleh said to them, "Do you not fear (Allah)
Of course I am a faithful (and a reliable) messenger for you
So fear Allah and obey me
In return, I do not seek any compensation from you. My reward exists only with the Lord of the universe
Would you be allowed to stay in these comforts, forever secure
In these gardens and springs
And the green fields, and date trees with their succulent fruit
You carve homes out of mountains skillfully
So fear Allah and follow me
Do not obey the orders of the immoderate (and the unrestrained)
Those who spoil the morals (and spread corruption and depravity) on the earth, and do nothing to improve matters
They said, "Surely, you are one of the crazy persons
You are just a human being like us! Bring us a sign if you are telling the truth
(The messenger Saleh) said, "Here, (the sign) is this camel. On specified days, the source of water shall be solely for the camel, while on other days it will be yours
Do not cause it any harm, or else the punishment of a severe day will grab you
But they killed the camel; a decision they came to regret
A torment gripped them. There is a sign in that, of course! But most of them do not believe
Your Lord is surely the One Who is the most Powerful and the most Merciful
The nation of Loot rejected the messengers
Their brother Loot said to them, "Do you not fear (Allah)
I am surely a faithful (and a reliable) messenger for you
So fear Allah and obey me
In return, I do not seek any compensation from you. My reward exists only with the Lord of the universe
Do you commit (the sexual act) with the males in this world
And you forsake the mates that your Lord created for you? Indeed, you are a nation guilty of transcending the limits
They said, "If you did not stop, oh Loot, you would most certainly be expelled
He said, "I am certainly among those who loathe and abhor your deeds
He prayed, "My Lord! Save me and my family from (the evil of) what they do
So We saved him and all of his family
Except an old woman, _ Loot´s wife _ who stayed behind (with the evil doers)
After that We annihilated the rest of them
We doused them with a downpour (of brimstone)! A devastating evil rain (fell) upon those forewarned
There is surely a sign in this! But most of them do not believe
Your Lord is surely the One Who is the most Powerful and the most Merciful
And the people of ´Aika´ rejected the messengers
When Shoaib said to them, "Do you not fear (Allah)
I am surely a faithful (and a reliable) messenger for you
So fear Allah and obey me
