Therefore, believe in Allah and His messenger; and the light (of revelation) which We have sent down. Allah is well Aware of what you do
The day of gathering _ that day when He will gather all of you together _ will be the day of loss and gain, (the day of reparation and redress of wrongful deeds). He (Allah) will remove (and cleanse) the shortcomings (and sins) of the one who believes in Allah, and does righteous acts. He will admit such a person into paradise to live forever; rivers run right through it. That is the greatest success
(While) those who disbelieve and deny Our signs, shall really be the companions of fire. They will live there forever! It is a despicable destination
Unless it is with the (will and) permission of Allah, no calamity can ever strike (anyone). Allah guides (and soothes) the heart of the one who believes in Him. Allah is well-Aware of every single thing
Obey Allah, and obey His messenger! (Bear this in mind) if you turn away, (that the responsibility) upon our messenger is (nothing more than) to convey the message clearly and plainly
Allah! There is no god except He! The believers should place their trust in Allah
Oh those of you who believe! Your enemies are (likely to be) among your spouses and your children. Beware of them! If you forego, forbear and forgive, (you will find that) Allah is indeed the most Forgiving and the most Merciful
In reality, your wealth and your children are a trial (for you). There exists with Allah, a tremendous tribute (at the end of the trial)
(Practice righteousness and restraint), and fear Allah as much as you can. Listen and obey, and give charity. It is for your own good. The successful ones are really those who escape the greed within their own selves
If you advance Allah a sincere loan, He will multiply it and return it to you twofold; and (in addition) He will grant you forgiveness. Allah is the most Forbearing; He appreciates (and rewards) gratitude
(He is) the Knower of the unseen and the manifest, the Almighty, the Wisest
Oh prophet, (and Oh you believers)! If you (must) divorce your women, divorce them for a (prescribed) period. Count the period (correctly). Fear Allah, your Lord, and do not _ unless they have committed a flagrantly immoral act _ expel your divorced women out of their homes. The women too should not leave their homes. These are the confines of Allah. Anyone overstepping the limits of Allah actually commits an outrage upon himself. You do not know! (During that period), Allah may well bring about something (to cause reconciliation between the husband and wife)
At the end of the (prescribed) period, either hold back your women (in wedlock) lawfully, according to the well-known (prescribed) manner, or make the divorce final in accordance with the well known (prescribed) way. Take two of your fair minded (and respected) men as your witnesses. (Oh witnesses)! Bear the witness truthfully for the sake of Allah! Those who believe in Allah, and the life-to-come, are hereby being asked to heed. Allah will provide a way out for the one who fears Him
And, He would grant the bounties (and provisions) from sources they had not expected (or even imagined). Allah is sufficient for anyone who places his trust in Him. (Always, and without an exception), Allah brings His decrees to destiny. Indeed, Allah it is Who has appointed the destiny for every single thing
(Remember), if you are in doubt about the ´iddat.´ of your women, _ either because they are past the age, or haven´t yet started to menstruate _ it lasts three months. The ´iddat´ for the pregnant women (is three months, or it) lasts till the termination of pregnancy. (iddat: the period after divorce during which a woman is forbidden to remarry). Allah (grants a leeway and) makes matters easy for the one who fears Him
This is the commandment of Allah; He has revealed it to you. Whoever fears Him (and practices righteousness and restraint), Allah will cleanse him of his sins (and rid him of his faults and flaws); and Allah will magnify his rewards
(During the period of ´iddat´) have the (divorced) women live where you live, as your resources allow. Do not abuse and mistreat them, in order to harass them. If they happen to be carrying (your) child, then spend and bear their expenses till they carry their pregnancies to term. If they are nursing (your child), then compensate them in a fair and equitable manner. Settle the issue (of compensation) between you and your (former) wives amicably. Should the matter (of compensation) be difficult (and hard to resolve), then any other woman may nurse the child
Let the well-to-do spend according to his means, and let the one with limited resources spend according to what Allah has granted him. Never does Allah obligate anyone in excess of what He has granted him. Allah may soon change the difficult circumstances into (leisure and) comfort
So many communities (in the past) have been insolent and arrogant towards the commandments of their Lord, and His messengers. So, very harshly We called them to account. We inflicted upon them a severe punishment
They tasted the evil consequences of their conduct. The final outcome of their conduct was (nothing but) sheer loss
For them, Allah has prepared the severest (most awful) punishment. So fear Allah, oh you endowed with reason and intellect; and (oh) those (of you) who believe! Allah has sent you a reminder (and an admonition)
A messenger recites for you the clear and unambiguous verses of Allah! So that he, (the messenger), may bring out of darkness into light, those who believe and act righteously. Allah will usher into paradise _ rivers run right through it _ anyone who believes in Him and performs righteous deeds. There, he will live forever and ever. (There), Allah has (kept in store) excellent (and everlasting) bounties for him
Allah has created the seven heavens. And the same goes for the earth! The commands (of Allah) prevail over all of them (constantly). So that you may know (for sure), that Allah is capable of doing everything; and that Allah has (full and unabridged) knowledge of every single thing
Oh prophet! Why did you, in order to please your wives, forbid yourself that which Allah has deemed lawful for you? Allah is all-Forgiving, the most Merciful
Allah has prescribed a procedure for you to expiate (and rescind) such oaths. Allah is your Patron; He is the most Knowledgeable, the Wisest
(Remember)! The prophet confided in one of his wives concerning a certain matter. When she divulged (the information) to another one (of his wives), Allah informed the prophet about it. The prophet told his wife a portion (of what Allah had informed him) and ignored the rest. When he told her about it, she asked, "Who told you about this?" He replied, "The One Who knows all and is the most Aware has told me
(Oh wives of the prophet), the two of you better turn to Allah and repent. Your hearts have wandered off the right path. But if you back each other against the prophet, then (beware)! Allah is certainly his friend! And so are the angel Gibraeel, and all the righteous believers. Besides that, all the angels are his supporters
In case the prophet divorces you all, his Lord would perhaps grant him other wives _ widows or maidens, in your place. They would be better than you, more obedient, believing, pious, penitent and fond of fasting
Oh you who believe, save yourselves and your families from the fire. Humans and stones are its fuel! Burly and rigidly fierce angels are (appointed as guards) over it. They do not disobey or disregard any of the commands of Allah. (Rather), they (diligently) carry out whatever they are commanded
Oh you unbelievers! Do not make excuses today. You are being punished only for what you have (actually) done (and nothing else)
Oh you believers! Turn to Allah in repentance, an earnest (and heartfelt) repentance. Allah, your Lord, may just rid you of your sins (and your faults and flaws); He will usher you into paradise, through which run the rivers. Allah will not let the prophet and those who believe in him, be humiliated on that day. The light (emanating from them) would run in front of, and to the right of them. They shall call out, "Our Lord, (please) complete for us our light, and forgive us. Indeed, You have power over all things
Oh prophet! Wage a relentless struggle against the unbelievers, and the hypocrites. Be stern against them (and do not yield). Hell shall be their abode! What an evil (despicable) destination
For the unbelievers, Allah cites the case of the wives of the prophets ´Nooh´ and ´Loot´. They were married to two of Our most honorable and righteous servants. But they betrayed their husbands, and so their husbands could not help them against Allah at all. Both of these women were ordered to enter the hellfire just like all the others who (deserved to enter hell, and) would live there for ever
And for the believers. Allah cites the example of the pharaoh´s wife. She said, "Lord, (please) build me a house in paradise under your (auspicious) care. Save me from the pharaoh and his (evil) deeds, and save me from (such) an unjust nation
(And the example of) Mary, a daughter Imran, who had (rigidly) guarded her chastity. We breathed Our spirit into her. Thus, she gave credence (and bore witness) to the words of her Lord and His scriptures. She was (truly) among the obedient ones
Blessed is the One Who holds in his hand the kingdom (of the heavens and the earth). He is capable of accomplishing everything
(Blessed is) the One Who created the death and life, so He may try and test you; which of you performs the better deeds. He is the most Powerful, and the most Kind
The One Who created seven tiers of heavens, one atop another! You do not find any disparity or disharmony in the creation of Rehman, (the most Merciful). Cast another look! Do you find any breach (in the heavens)
(Go ahead)! Look again and again. Your eyes would wear out, and your sight would (wander and) return to you, bewildered and in vain
We have embellished the heaven nearest to this world with (numerous) lamps (the stars). We have made this heaven (a means) to bombard the Shaitan with missiles, to drive them away. For them, We have prepared a punishment by the blazing fire
There exists a punishment of hell for those who refuse to believe in their Lord. Theirs is a despicable destination
As they are hurled into hell, they would hear it shriek and scream (in anger); it would boil over furiously, as it blazes
It would almost explode in its frenzied fury. As a fresh crop (of sinners) is flung into hell, its warden would ask, "(How did you end up here)? Hadn´t a warner come to you
They would reply, "Yes! A warner had indeed come to us, but (alas)! We rejected him and said: "Allah has revealed nothing! You have just (blundered and) slumped into a grave error
They would say, "Had we listened (attentively), or applied our mind, we would have escaped being the inmates of the blazing fire
Thus, they would confess their sins; damned are the inmates of the fiery flames
Forgiveness and a rich reward exists for those who fear their Lord, though they do not see Him
(Little does it matter whether you) whisper your words in secret, or shout them out aloud! He is indeed aware of everything, (every thought) that passes through the heart
Why would He not know? He is the Creator! He is the all-Knowing, well Aware of every subtle detail
He it is, Who subdued the earth for you (and made it a comfortable and controllable habitat). So move along its surface and eat the food provided by Him. But (remember), towards Him is your (revival and) resurrection
Are you unafraid that He, the One in heavens (Allah), will not let the earth swallow you? That it will not suddenly begin to rock (as in an earthquake)
Are you unafraid that He _the One in heaven, (Allah) _will not unleash a violent hurricane upon you? Then you would learn in a hurry how (true and terrible) was My warning
Of course, (most of) their predecessors had (also) refused to believe. So (observe), how (devastating) was My wrath (and punishment)
Do they not look at the birds above them? They flap and fold their wings (and fly)! No one but Rehman, (the Merciful), holds them up (in mid air). Indeed He is the One watching over every single thing
Do you have an army that can support you against the Merciful (Lord)? In fact, the unbelievers are just duped by a delusion
If He withholds His bounties from you, do you have anyone else who could grant you the provisions? The fact is, they hide behind their pride, and their (irrational) aversion (to the truth)
So who (do you think) is better guided? The one crawling on his face groping (to find his way), or the one walking upright along the straight path
Say, "It is He Who brought you into being, and conferred upon you (the faculties of) hearing, sight and reasoning. Seldom do you express gratitude
Say, "It is He Who has spread you across the earth; and (in the end) you would be summoned back to Him
They say, "When will that promise come to be, if you are truthful
Say, "That knowledge lies solely with Allah; in fact I am simply a warner
Actually, the faces of the unbelievers would distort (with horror) when they witness the torment in close proximity. They would be told "(this is the promise), this is what you had called for
Say, "Have you thought it over? Regardless of whether Allah destroys me and my companions, or shows us His mercy, (the question before you should be) who will shelter the unbelievers from the painful punishment
Say, "He is Rehman, (the most Merciful). We believe in Him! And in Him we trust. Very soon, you will find out who has committed the obvious (and the gravest) blunder
Say, "Have you thought it over? Should (all) your (drinking) water sink underground (and disappear), who can supply you with springs and clean running water (to drink)
Nun! (Allah swears by) the pen and whatever they, (the angels), write
(Oh prophet), you are not, by the grace of your Lord, a mad man
In fact, you certainly have a perpetual and ever lasting reward (with your Lord)
Indeed, you certainly bear the highest moral character
Soon you will see, and so shall they
Who is deranged _ (you or they)
Indeed, your Lord knows well who has strayed from His path; and He (also) knows those who are the rightly guided
Do not yield to those who have denied the truth
They would love it if you make concessions (and compromise the truth somewhat). They too, would then give in (some)
And do not obey the contemptible oath-monger
The abusive mudslinger, who throws insults around (all the time)
The one who prohibits the good, trespasses and defiantly indulges in sinful acts
Ignoble and greedy, in short, despised
(He acts that way), because he is wealthy and has (many) children
When Our verses are recited to him, he remarks, "(Legends)! Tales of the earlier folks
Very soon, We will (burn and) brand his snout
Indeed, We have put them through a test, just as We tested the owners of an orchard. They swore to pick its fruit the next morning
They allowed no exception, (They did not say, "If Allah pleases)
So, while they slept, a calamity from their Lord visited that orchard (and destroyed it completely)
By the morning, it looked bare, as if it had already been picked clean
At daybreak they called each other
Proceed to your field early in the morning, if you want to pick the fruit (today)
So they departed, muttering to each other
Today, do not let the poor and the needy enter the orchard and pester you (for alms)
With that resolve, and certain (in their minds) that they had the means (to harvest), they left in the morning
When they saw their orchard, they (failed to recognize it, and) cried out, "We have surely lost our way
No! Rather, we have been deprived
The moderate one among them said, "Did I not tell you? Why did you not chant (your Lord´s) praises
They said, "Exalted is our Lord. In fact, we were the wrongdoers
Then they turned around, and began blaming each other
They said, "Indeed, we had certainly acted arrogantly
Hopefully, our Lord will grant us something better in its place. Of course, we do turn to our Lord for forgiveness
Such is the punishment (in this life), but the torment of the afterlife is far greater, if they only knew
For the righteous, there exist with their Lord the blessings filled gardens
Are We to treat the obedient ones the same as the criminals
What is wrong with you? How do you draw your conclusions
Or did you learn it from your scriptures
That you shall have whatever you prefer
Or, do you hold a binding contract over Us till the day of Resurrection, (guaranteeing) that whatever you order shall be yours
Ask them. Who amongst them can claim that
Or, do they have (other gods as Allah´s) partners (offering them such a guarantee)? Let them produce these partners if they are truthful
They would be asked to prostrate (before Allah) on that day when the reality is laid bare. But (that day), they shall find themselves unable (to prostrate)
Downcast would be their eyes (in shame); disgrace shall overwhelm them. They were asked to prostrate in this life, when they were sound and solid
So let Me handle (all) those who reject this Qur´an. Gradually, We would lead them (into Hell), by means they would seldom perceive
I will let them have a little respite. My scheme is a cinch _ (airtight and foolproof)
Or, do you ask them for a fee (or a reward)? Are they laboring under the burden (of such a demand)
Or, do they have the knowledge of the unseen so they may write (their own fate)
So, wait patiently for your Lord´s decree. Do not act like the man of the fish, (the prophet Jonah), when he called (his Lord), choked with grief
(In the fish he would still be), had the mercy of your Lord not reached him. He was tossed on the bare (and barren) beach _ censured (and chastised)
Eventually, his Lord chose him and placed him among the righteous ones
The unbelievers look at you with aversion (and animosity), and they almost trip you up with their eyes. They hear this reminder, the Qur´an, and say, "He is really a man possessed
Although it is (nothing but) a reminder for the whole world
The Reality
And what is (that inevitable) Reality
What do you understand by the ´Reality´
The ´Samoods´ and the ´Aads´ denied the (impending) calamity of sudden onset _ (the hour of Judgment)
So the Samoods were wiped out by the lightning (and the thunderbolt)
While the ´Aads´ were destroyed by the violent howling winds
For seven hideous days and eight gruesome nights, He let the winds ravage them. (Had you been there), you could see their bodies tossed about (and strewn around), as if they were the hollowed out trunks of the date trees
Do you see any of them around, anymore
The pharaoh, and those before him _ the overturned cities (of Sodom and Gomorrah) _ committed the (very same) crime
They defied the messengers of their Lord, and so He seized (and squeezed) them into a tight grip
Indeed, (oh believers, during the great deluge of Nooh) when the water began to inundate, We carried you (and kept you afloat) aboard a ship
So as to make it a memorable event for you; so that the attentive souls may retain an indelible memory of that event in their (subconscious) mind
As (soon as) the trumpet sounds for the first time
The earth and the mountains would be dislodged and crushed with a single blow
And so, on that day the inevitable (event) would come to pass
Feeble and frail, on that day the sky shall burst asunder
The angels would be present there, at the edge (of the throne). Eight of them would carry your Lord´s throne above them
That shall be the day you are presented before Him (with all your secrets bared); none of your intimate secrets shall remain unexposed
Then, the one who is given his record (of deeds) in his right hand would say, (excitedly to others), "Here, take (a look)! Read the record (of my deeds)
I really did believe that (one day), I would have to face the reckoning
So, he shall have a pleasant and blissful (ever lasting) life
In the exalted (gardens of delight)
With its cluster of fruit (drooping low), within easy reach
(Enjoy)! Eat and drink (and relish your reward), the result of the deeds you had earned in the life gone by
While he, who is given his record (of deeds) in his left hand would (lament and) say, "I wish I had never been given my record
I wish I had never known (the contents of) my record
I wish my death (in the world) had been final (and decisive)
My wealth (and possessions) did not help me
And my (talents and) faculties have (waned and) gone

Indeed, We sent Nooh towards his people (and said to him), "Warn your people before (it is too late, and) a painful punishment befalls them
He said, "Oh my people, I am obviously a messenger towards you
(With a message) that you should worship Allah (exclusively); you should fear Him, and obey me

But my calls have only increased their hatred (for the truth)

Indeed, I (not only) declared (and conveyed the message) to them in public, (but) I even reasoned with them in private

He will send abundant rain for you from the sky
He will help you and cause you to increase in wealth and offspring. He will grant you gardens. He will cause rivers to flow (in your land)
What is the matter with you? Why do you not expect (and anticipate) dignity from Allah
He has created you in stages

Allah has laid the earth out for you as a wide expanse
So you move about in this world, over highways and mountain passes

They have hatched a mighty awesome scheme

Nooh prayed, "My Lord, do not leave any one of them (alive) on (the surface of) the earth

Indeed, He _ Exalted and Majestic as He is _ did not (ever) take a mate or a son

And people thought _ as you did _ that Allah will not resurrect anyone
We scanned (and surveyed) the sky and found it teaming with watchful guards and flaming meteors

Of course, we did not know whether a (cosmic) calamity has been planned for those on earth, or that their Lord intends to reveal to them the right path
Among us (jinn), there are some that are righteous, and others that are quite the opposite. We follow diverse (and divergent) paths
We have come to realize that we will never (be able to) evade Allah on earth. Nor can we ever evade Him if we run away (and leave the earth)
In fact, when we heard the guidance, we believed it. Thus, whoever believes in his Lord never needs to worry about his (good) deeds losing their worth. Nor shall he ever fear an injustice
Indeed, some of us (have surrendered and) are obedient, while others have deviated (from the right path). In fact, those accepting Islam (as their way of life) are really the ones seeking the right path

You may recite as much of the Qur´an as you easily can. He knows that (at any given time) some of you would be sick, and others would be travelling in search of Allah´s bounties. No, of course not! Man is surely rebellious
For, he thinks he is independent
(Even though his final) return is towards your Lord
Did you (oh Muhammad, SAW), see the one who forbids
The servant (of Allah) to perform ´salat´
What do you think? Is he well guided
And (does he) enjoin piety
Or do you think he denied and turned away
Does he not know that Allah watches (everything)
Of course not! If he did not desist, We will surely drag him by the hair on his forehead
The lying sinful lock of hair
He may then call his henchmen for help
While, We shall summon the guardians of hell
No! Beware! Do not follow such a one. (Rather), fall prostrate and draw closer (to Allah)
Certainly, We have revealed it _ (the Qur´an) _ in the Night of Decree
And what do you understand by the Night of Decree
The Night of Power is better than a thousand months
Bearing the divine decrees, the angels and the spirits descend during the night with the permission of their Lord
Blissful and serene is that night, right until the day breaks
Those of the people of the scriptures and the polytheists who do not believe, will not give up (disbelief) until the clear evidence comes to them
The messenger of Allah recites from the sacred and sanctified scripture _ (the Qur´an)
Containing sound and straightforward rules
Those given the (earlier) scriptures (argued and) differed amongst themselves after clear proofs had already come to them
What they were commanded was to worship only Allah with sincerity and exclusive devotion; and to worship nothing and nobody else with Him. (They were ordered) to establish ´salat´, and to pay the ´zakat´. That is truly the stable (and established) religion
Whoever denies among the people of the book and the polytheists, would be in the fire of hell, and would stay there forever. Such are the worst of the creation
While those who believe and do good deeds are certainly the best of the creation
Their reward, the paradise of Eden _ rivers run right through it _ is with their Lord. They shall live there forever. Allah is pleased with them, and they with Him! This is for the one who fears his Lord
When the earth is shaken up with a cataclysmic quake
And the earth yields and disgorges (all) its burden
And man remarks, "What is the matter with it
That day, it will recount all that ever occurred on it
For, your Lord shall have ordered it (to do so)
On that day, people will come out (of their graves) separately, so they may be shown (the result of) their deeds
Then, whoever did (even) an atom´s worth of good, shall see it
And whoever commits an atom´s worth of evil, shall see it
(I swear by) these panting snorting horses
Striking sparks (with their hooves)
Dashing to assault by dawn
Kicking up clouds of dust
And storming blindly into the crowds
Man is indeed ungrateful to his Lord
And to that fact, he is himself a witness
He surely loves wealth and riches with a passion
Does he not know, that when all the contents of the graves are disgorged
And all the secrets buried in the hearts are divulged
That day, (they would learn that) their Lord is thoroughly Knowledgeable about their deeds
That awesome (stunning) disaster
What is (that) awesome disaster
What do you suppose is that awesome disaster
That day, people would be like scattered (confused) moths
And the mountains like the fluffy tufts of colored wool
Anyone whose scales (of good deeds) weigh heavier
Would live in a state of bliss
As for the one whose scale (of good deeds) is lighter
An abysmal pit would totally engulf him
And what do you think is (the content of) the abysmal pit
Hot blazing fire
(Oh men! Your obsession to attain, hoard and show off) opulence diverts you (and keeps you busy)
Right until you land in (your) graves
No, surely not! You shall soon find out
Again, be sure! You shall soon find out
No, of course not! If you only knew with certainty
You shall surely see hell
Then, you would really see it with the eye of certainty
And then, you would certainly be called to account for the blessings and the bounties
(I swear) by Time
Indeed, mankind happens to be in a state of a grave loss
Except for those who believe, perform good deeds, strive for the truth, and strive with patience and perseverance
Misery is for the slanderer and the backbiter
The one who gathers wealth; and counts it (zestfully)
And thinks that his wealth confers immortality
Of course not! He will certainly be flung into the ´Wrecker´
And what do you suppose is the ´Wrecker´
(It is) the fire of Allah, kindled ablaze
Which will rise (and reach) up to (clutch) the hearts
Indeed, an inverted dome (of fire) would be (placed) upon them
Enclosed in (a fence of) tall pillars
Are you not aware of how your Lord dealt with the army accompanied by the elephants
Did He not make their (evil) plans go awry
He let loose upon them a large flock of birds
That pelted them with pellets made of baked clay
Thus, He turned them into the chewed out chaff
(The tribe of) Quraish is well known
Renowned for their summer and winter journeys
They should (devotedly) worship the Lord of this house (the ´Kaaba´ in Makkah)
Who feeds them, and protects them from (famine and) hunger. And secures them from (danger and) fear
Haven´t you seen the one who rejects the fact of the reward and punishment
He is (really) the one who (shoos and) shoves away the orphans harshly
And does not promote the feeding of the poor
Of course, misery is for (some of) those who perform ´salat´
Those among them who stay unmindful of their "salat´
Those who aim to be seen (doing good)
And they hold back even minor favors
For sure, We granted you (excellence and) abundance
So pray only to your Lord, and offer sacrifice
For anyone who hates you, will be cut off (from your Lord´s mercy)
Say, "Oh you unbelievers
That which you worship is not what I worship
And you are not going to worship the One that I worship
I shall never worship that which you serve so devotedly
Nor will you worship Whom I worship
You have your faith, and I have mine
Once Allah´s help _ and with it, the victory _ arrives
You shall see people throng (and embrace) the religion of Allah in large numbers
So chant the praises of your Lord, and beg His forgiveness. Of course, it is really He Who accepts repentance and grants forgiveness
May the hands of Abu Lahab _ (an uncle of the Prophet) _ perish; and so may he
(All) his wealth, and everything he has earned failed him
Soon, he will roast in the blazing fire
And his woman, that tale-bearing malicious gossip
Shall have a rope of palm fibers around her neck
Say "He _ (Allah) _ is One, (the most Unique)
Allah is the Self-sufficient Master _ (the Ultimate Source, the Uncaused Cause)
He did not beget, and He was not begotten
And, there is absolutely no one equal to Him; no one is even remotely comparable
Say, "I seek refuge with (Allah), the Lord of the nascent dawn
From the evil He has created
From the evil of darkness as it deepens (during the night)
From the evil of (women practicing) witchcraft, and blowing (spells) over knotted ropes
And from the evil of the grudgeful, as he turns green with jealousy
Say, "I seek refuge with the Lord of mankind
The King of mankind
The God of mankind
(I seek refuge) from the evil of the devil _ (the whispering tempter)
The one who (breathes doubts and) whispers in the hearts of mankind
Amongst the jinn and the human kind
